<DESCRIPTION>PRESS RELEASE
<TEXT>

    <body bgcolor="#ffffff" style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><br>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Exhibit
99.1</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="right">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right" align="left"><img src="acl6k0309allegretto0.jpg" alt=""></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon
Signs Contract with LCA-Vision for 75 <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">ALLEGRETTO WAVE</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super; FONT-STYLE: italic">&#174;
</font>Excimer Lasers</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">LASIK
chain standardizes with high-end technology based on study results.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">HUENENBERG, Switzerland</font> <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#8211; March 10, 2009 &#8211; </font>Alcon, Inc.
(NYSE: ACL) announced today that its affiliate Alcon Laboratories, Inc. has
signed a five year contract with LCA-Vision, Inc. (NASDAQ: LCAV). Under the
contract, LCA will place ALLEGRETTO WAVE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> Eye-Q
400Hz excimer lasers in all of the company&#8217;s 75 Lasik<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Plus</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> vision
surgery centers by the end of the third quarter of 2009. The contract comes as
part of a decision by LCA to standardize its laser surgery technology on two
laser platforms based on the results of a clinical study.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>&#8220;Lasik<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Plus</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> recently
completed a contralateral, prospective, randomized study measuring surgical
outcomes on a variety of excimer lasers, including the most recently
FDA-approved laser, the ALLEGRETTO WAVE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> Eye-Q,&#8221;
said Steven C. Straus, chief executive officer of LCA-Vision. &#8220;The ALLEGRETTO
WAVE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> Eye-Q
excimer laser performed well on our evaluation criteria, leading to our decision
to reduce our laser platforms from three to two and to expand our relationship
with Alcon.&#8221;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>Conducted through cooperation between
members of the LCA medical advisory board and an outside research consultant,
the study compared the clinical outcomes of laser eye surgery on various lasers.
Results demonstrated excellent clinical outcomes on the ALLEGRETTO WAVE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> Eye-Q
excimer laser.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8220;We are
excited about the positive results of this clinical trial, which led to this
agreement and the opportunity it provides Alcon to expand our relationship with
LCA-Vision,&#8221; said Bill Barton, U.S. area president at Alcon. &#8220;The study
validates the investment we made in WaveLight and clearly demonstrates the
quality outcomes achieved by the Allegretto platform.&#8221;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon&#8217;s
ALLEGRETTO WAVE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174; </font>Eye-Q
excimer laser combines proprietary wavefront-optimized PerfectPulse
Technology<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font>, precise
laser control and unparalleled speed for the most advanced laser technology in
LASIK surgery. Alcon acquired the U.S. rights to the technology through the
acquisition of assets from WaveLight AG in February of 2008.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About
ALLEGRETTO WAVE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font>
Eye-Q</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Alcon
ALLEGRETTO WAVE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> Eye-Q
excimer laser, engineered by WaveLight AG, combines precision technology with
excellent laser energy stability, high-quality components and reliability. Built
with pioneering wavefront principles, the laser&#8217;s PerfectPulse Technology<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> is
designed to control each laser pulse from its generation to the exact point
where it contacts the cornea.&#160; The ALLEGRETTO WAVE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> Eye-Q
Excimer laser platform is the fastest laser in the United States at 400Hz and
aims to provide optimal LASIK results.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About
Alcon</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon,
Inc. is the world&#8217;s leading eye care company, with sales of approximately $6.3
billion in 2008.&#160;&#160;Alcon, which has been dedicated to the ophthalmic
industry for 60 years, researches, develops, manufactures and markets
pharmaceuticals, surgical equipment and devices, contact lens care solutions and
other vision care products that treat diseases, disorders and other conditions
of the eye. Alcon is the majority shareholder of WaveLight
AG.&#160;&#160;&#160;For more information on Alcon, Inc., visit the Company&#8217;s
web site at www.alcon.com.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"># #
